    >

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

<script>
(function () {
  function updateBadge(container) {
    const card = container.closest('.product-card') || container.closest('[data-product], [data-product-card]') || container;
    const badge = card && card.querySelector('.product-badges__badge--rectangle');
    if (!badge) return;

    const hasCompare = !!container.querySelector('.compare-at-price');
    badge.classList.toggle('badge--hidden', !hasCompare);
  }

  // initial pass (grid + PDP)
  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(updateBadge);

  // watch for price changes (variant selects, ajax renders, etc.)
  const mo = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    const touched = new Set();
    mutations.forEach(m => {
      const container = (m.target.closest && m.target.closest('[ref="priceContainer"]')) || null;
      if (container && !touched.has(container)) {
        touched.add(container);
        updateBadge(container);
      }
    });
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
    mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  });

  // if cards are added later (infinite scroll, quick view, etc.), re-scan
  const moBody = new MutationObserver(() => {
    document.querySelectorAll('[ref="priceContainer"]').forEach(node => {
      // only attach if not already observed (cheap check via dataset flag)
      if (!node.dataset._capWatch) {
        node.dataset._capWatch = '1';
        updateBadge(node);
        mo.observe(node, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      }
    });
  });
  moBody.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();

</script>

    <script>
      (() => {
        const header = document.getElementById('header-component');
        if (!header) return;

        // Hysteresis band (prevents flicker)
        const ENTER_TOP_AT = 60; // when scrolling up: become "top" at <= 60px
        const EXIT_TOP_AT = 140; // when scrolling down: leave "top" only after > 140px

        let isTop = true; // current state
        let ticking = false;

        const apply = () => {
          const y = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop || 0;

          // Only switch state when we clearly crossed the band edges
          if (isTop && y > EXIT_TOP_AT) isTop = false;
          else if (!isTop && y <= ENTER_TOP_AT) isTop = true;

          header.toggleAttribute('data-at-top', isTop);
          ticking = false;
        };

        const onScroll = () => {
          if (ticking) return;
          ticking = true;
          requestAnimationFrame(apply);
        };

        // Init
        apply();
        window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
        window.addEventListener('resize', onScroll);
      })();
    </script>
